people_list=[]
part_1 = 'https://telescope.epam.com/rest/e3s-eco-scripting-impl/0.1.0/data/searchFts?metaType=meta:people-suite:people-api:com.epam.e3s.app.people.api.data.pluggable.EmployeeEntity&query=%7B%22statements%22%3A%5B%7B%22query%22%3A%22*%22%7D%5D%2C%22filters%22%3A%5B%5D%2C%22start%22%3A'
part_2 = '%2C%22limit%22%3A100%2C%22entity%22%3A%22meta%3Apeople-suite%3Apeople-api%3Acom.epam.e3s.app.people.api.data.pluggable.EmployeeEntity%22%7D'

for index in range(0,41200,100):
    r = requests.get(part_1 + str(index) + part_2
                ,cookies = {'JSESSIONID':'hgb0q4ezxwzl7we7pxy61b17',
                            'mellon-telescope-aws-production':'0a690ae95ec5ed331eabf8c1dc46477a',
                            'ROUTEID':'telescope.telescope0'})
    if r.status_code == 200:
        for i in r.json()['items']:
            people_list.append(i['data'])
    else:
        print(index)
        break
        
    print('parse', index)

heroes_list=[]
part_1 = 'https://telescope.epam.com/eco/rest/e3s-eco-scripting-impl/0.1.0/data/select?metaType=meta:hero-suite:people-hero-api:com.epam.e3s.app.people.hero.api.data.HeroEntity&start='
part_2 = '&limit=5000&query={}'

for index in range(0,350001,5000):
    r = requests.get(part_1 + str(index) + part_2
                ,cookies = {'JSESSIONID':'hgb0q4ezxwzl7we7pxy61b17',
                            'mellon-telescope-aws-production':'0a690ae95ec5ed331eabf8c1dc46477a',
                            'ROUTEID':'telescope.telescope0'})
    if r.status_code == 200:
        for i in r.json():
            heroes_list.append(i)
    else:
        print(index)
        break
        
    print('parse', index)

In [59]:
assignmentIds = []
assignerTypes = []
badgeIds = []
fromNames = []
fromIds = []
dates = []
comments = []
upsaIds = []
In [60]:
for rec in heroes_loaded_list:
    for badge in rec.get('bean').get('badge'):
        assignmentIds.append(badge.get('assignmentId'))
        assignerTypes.append(badge.get('assignerType'))
        badgeIds.append(badge.get('id'))
        fromNames.append(badge.get('fromName'))
        fromIds.append(badge.get('fromId'))
        dates.append(badge.get('date'))
        comments.append(badge.get('comment'))
        upsaIds.append(rec.get('bean').get('upsaId'))
In [61]:
heroes_df = pd.DataFrame({'assignmentId': assignmentIds,
                         'assignerType': assignerTypes,
                         'badgeId': badgeIds,
                         'fromName': fromNames,
                         'fromId': fromIds,
                         'date': dates,
                         'comment': comments,
                         'upsaId': upsaIds})
